<p style="margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;text-indent:7.69%;">14</a></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU15"></a><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">REVOLVING CREDIT NOTE</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">U.S.$20,000,000.00</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">1.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">PROMISE TO PAY/PLACE OF PAYMENT</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;FOR VALUE RECEIVED, the undersigned KURA SUSHI USA INC., a Delaware corporation, (&#8220;Borrower&#8221;), promises to pay KURA SUSHI INC., a Japanese corporation (&#8220;Lender&#8221;), the principal sum of Twenty Million United States Dollars (U.S.$20,000,000.00), or such lesser sum as may be loaned to Borrower pursuant to the Loan Agreement (as defined below), together with interest on the principal balance, from time to time remaining unpaid, from the Disbursement Date until paid, at the Interest Rate set forth in this Note.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">2.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">RECORD OF ADVANCES AND CREDIT.</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower hereby authorizes Lender to enter in its books and records all loans (&#8220;Advances&#8221;) made to Borrower and all payments of principal amounts in respect of such loans, which entries shall, in the absence of manifest error, be conclusive as to the outstanding principal amount of all loans made to Borrower; provided, however that the failure to make such entries with respect to any loan or payment shall not limit or otherwise affect the obligations of Borrower under the Loan Agreement or this Note.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">3.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">DEFINITIONS</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Capitalized terms in this Note that are not defined when first used have the meanings set forth below or, if not defined below, as defined in the Loan Agreement:</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">3.1<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Disbursement Date</font><font style="font-weight:normal;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Disbursement Date is the date on which Lender first disburses an Advance to or for the account of Borrower.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">3.2<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Interest Rate</font><font style="font-weight:normal;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Interest Rate shall be _____________ (___%) per annum.&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">3.3<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Loan Agreement</font><font style="font-weight:normal;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Loan Agreement is that certain revolving credit agreement of even date herewith, between Lender and Borrower, as the same may be amended from time to time.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU16"></a>3.4<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Prime Rate.</font><font style="font-weight:normal;color:#000000;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Prime Rate shall mean the rate of interest which Bank of America, N.A. (&#8220;BOA&#8221;) announces and publishes from its principal office in San Francisco as its &#8220;prime rate&#8221;.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Prime Rate is not intended to be the lowest rate of interest charged by BOA to its borrowers.&nbsp;&nbsp;Each change in the Interest Rate shall become effective on the effective date of each change in Prime Rate, as announced by BOA.&nbsp;&nbsp;If more than one category of &#8220;prime rate&#8221; publicly announced by BOA is in effect during any calendar month, the Prime Rate shall be the highest &#8220;prime rate&#8221; in effect.&nbsp;&nbsp;If </font></p>
<p style="margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;text-indent:7.69%;">15</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-weight:normal;color:#000000;">BOA shall not publicly announce its &#8220;prime rate&#8221;, then the Prime Rate shall be the highest reference, base or prime rate in effect as announced by the largest bank (in terms of capital and surplus) having its principal office in Los Angeles, California, which bank publicly announces such a rate</font><font style="font-weight:normal;color:#000000;">.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">4.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">PAYMENT OF PRINCIPAL AND INTEREST</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Principal and interest shall be payable in accordance with the following provisions:</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">4.1<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Payments of Interest</font><font style="font-weight:normal;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower shall pay to Lender interest on the unpaid principal balance of this Note, on demand, at the then prevailing Interest Rate.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower and Lender agree that the Interest Rate on an Advance may be subject to adjustment by mutual agreement if the maturity of an Advance is renewed or extended. </font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">4.2<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Application of Payments</font><font style="font-weight:normal;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Notwithstanding any provision to the contrary, payments of principal and interest received shall be applied first to any late payment fees, then to accrued interest, and lastly to principal.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">4.3<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Payments of Principal</font><font style="font-weight:normal;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower shall repay each cash Advance not later than the date which is twelve (12) months after the date of the initial disbursement thereof, unless Lender and Borrower agree on the extension of the maturity thereof for an additional period of twelve (12) months.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">5.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">CALCULATION OF INTEREST</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Interest payable with respect to any monthly payment shall be calculated according to the actual number of days in such period as a fraction of a 360&#8209;day year.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">6.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">PREPAYMENTS WITH NO PENALTY</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower may at any time prepay the principal amount outstanding under this Note in whole or in part together with accrued interest to the date of such prepayment on the amount prepaid.&nbsp;&nbsp;Amounts prepaid hereunder may be re-borrowed.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">7.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">ACCELERATION ON DEFAULT</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;If any part of the principal or interest under this Note is not paid when due, or if an Event of Default under the Loan Agreement or any other instrument securing or executed in connection with this Note or the Loan Agreement is not cured by a date specified in a notice to Borrower, the entire principal amount outstanding and the accrued interest shall at once become due and payable at the option of Lender.&nbsp;&nbsp;Lender may exercise this option to accelerate during any Event of Default by Borrower regardless of any prior forbearance.&nbsp;&nbsp;Any failure of Lender to make such election following an Event of Default shall not constitute a waiver of Lender&#8217;s right to make the election in the event of any subsequent Event of Default.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU17"></a>8.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">LATE PAYMENT CHARGE</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;If any payment of principal or interest under this Note is not paid within five (5) calendar days of when due, a late charge of Two Hundred Dollars (US$200.00) may be charged by Lender for the purpose of defraying the expenses incident to handling such delinquent payments.&nbsp;&nbsp;Such late charge represents a reasonable sum considering all of the circumstances existing on the date </font></p>
<p style="margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;text-indent:7.69%;">16</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">of this Note and represents a fair and reasonable estimate of the costs that will be sustained by Lender due to the failure of Borrower to make timely payments.&nbsp;&nbsp;The parties further agree that proof of actual damages would be costly or inconvenient.&nbsp;&nbsp;Such late charge shall be paid without prejudice to the right of Lender to collect any other amounts provided to be paid or to declare a default under this Note or from exercising any of the other rights and remedies of Lender.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">9.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">INTEREST ON LATE PAYMENTS</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Notwithstanding any provision in this Note to the contrary, any principal, accrued interest, late payment charges, and other amounts which are payable under this Note, the Loan Agreement or any other instrument, agreement, or document executed by Borrower in connection with the loan evidenced by this Note and which are not paid within five (5) calendar days of when due, shall thereafter bear interest, compounded monthly, at the rate which is the sum of three percent (3%) per annum plus the Prime Rate then in effect, not to exceed the maximum rate of interest allowed by law.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">10.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">ATTORNEYS&#8217; FEES</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower agrees to pay the following costs, expenses, and attorneys&#8217; fees paid or incurred by Lender, or adjudged by a court:&nbsp;&nbsp;(1) Actual costs of collection, costs and expenses, and attorneys&#8217; fees paid or incurred in connection with the collection, enforcement, modification, or administration of this Note or any Loan Document, whether or not suit is filed; and (2) costs of suit and such sum as the court may adjudge as attorneys&#8217; fees in any action to enforce payment of this Note or any part of it.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition to the foregoing award of attorneys&#8217; fees, Lender shall be entitled to its attorneys&#8217; fees incurred in any post-judgment proceedings to enforce any judgment in connection with this Note or any Loan Document.&nbsp;&nbsp;This provision is separate and several and shall survive the merger of this provision into any judgment.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">11.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">WAIVER OF PRESENTMENT, NOTICE OF DISHONOR, AND PROTEST</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Presentment, notice of dishonor, and protest are waived by all makers, sureties, guarantors, and endorsers of this Note.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">12.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">FORBEARANCE NOT A WAIVER</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;No delay or omission on the part of Lender in exercising any rights under this Note or under the Loan Agreement or any other security agreement given to secure this Note, on default by Borrower, shall operate as a waiver of such right or of any other right under this Note or other agreements, for the same default or any other default.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower, any sureties, guarantors, and endorsers of this Note consent to all extensions without notice for any period or periods of time and to the acceptance of partial payments before or after maturity, and to the acceptance, release, and substitution of security, all without prejudice to Lender.&nbsp;&nbsp;Lender shall similarly have the right to deal in any way, at any time, with one or more of the foregoing parties without notice to any other party, and to grant such party any extensions of time for payments of any of the indebtedness, or to grant any other indulgences or forbearances whatsoever, without notice to any other party and without in any way affecting the personal liability of any such party.</font></p>
<p style="margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;text-indent:7.69%;">17</a></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU18"></a><font style="font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">13.</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">LOSS, THEFT, DESTRUCTION OR MUTILATION OF NOTE</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;In the event of the loss, theft or destruction of this Note, upon Borrower&#8217;s receipt of a reasonably satisfactory indemnification agreement executed in favor of Borrower by the party who held this Note immediately prior to its loss, theft or destruction, or in the event of the mutilation of this Note, upon Lender&#8217;s surrender to Borrower of the mutilated Note, Borrower shall execute and deliver to such party or Lender, as the case may be, a new promissory note in form and content identical to this Note in lieu of the lost, stolen, destroyed or mutilated Note.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">14.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">NOTICES</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Any notice, request, demand, statement, authorization, approval, or consent required or permitted under this Note shall be in writing and shall be made in accordance with Section 9.5 of the Loan Agreement.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">15.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">GOVERNING LAW.&nbsp;&nbsp;THIS NOTE SHALL BE CONSTRUED AND ENFORCEABLE ACCORDING TO THE LAWS OF THE STATE OF CALIFORNIA.&nbsp;&nbsp;VENUE FOR PURPOSES OF THIS NOTE WILL BE IN ANY COURT SERVICING ORANGE COUNTY AND BORROWER AGREES TO BE SUBJECT TO THE PERSONAL JURISDICTION OF THE STATE OF CALIFORNIA, INCLUDING ANY STATE OR FEDERAL COURT SITTING THEREIN AND ALL COURT RULES THEREOF.&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">16.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">WAIVER OF STATUTE OF LIMITATIONS</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;The pleading of any statute of limitations as a defense to the obligations evidenced by this Note is waived to the fullest extent permissible by law.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">17.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">TIME IS OF THE ESSENCE</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Time is of the essence for each and every obligation under this Note.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">18.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">ASSIGNMENT</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Lender shall have the right to sell, assign, or otherwise transfer, either in part or in its entirety, this Note, and any other instrument evidencing or securing the indebtedness of this Note without Borrower&#8217;s consent.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower may not assign or otherwise transfer this Note without Lender&#8217;s prior written consent.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:normal;font-variant: normal;">19.<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-transform:none;color:#000000;">SUCCESSORS AND ASSIGNS</font><font style="font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;This Note and all of the covenants, promises, and agreements contained in it shall be binding on and inure to the benefit of the respective legal and personal representatives, devises, heirs, successors, and assigns of Lender and Borrower.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;text-indent:7.69%;">18</a></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-family:'Times New Roman';"><font style="font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-family:'Times New Roman';">&#10146;</font></p></td>

<div align="left">

<td valign="top" style="width:3.85%;white-space:nowrap">

<td valign="top" style="width:3.85%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-family:'Times New Roman';"><font style="font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-family:'Times New Roman';">&#10146;</font></p></td>

<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri;">Restaurant-level contribution* was $3.9 million, compared to $2.9 million in the second quarter of 2019; and</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.85%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.85%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-family:'Times New Roman';"><font style="font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-family:'Times New Roman';">&#10146;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri;">Adjusted EBITDA* was $1.4 million, compared to $1.2 million in the second quarter of 2019.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:1.54%;text-indent:-1.54%;font-style:italic;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">* Restaurant-level contribution and Adjusted EBITDA are non-GAAP measures and are defined below under &#8220;Key Financial Definitions&#8221;. Please see the reconciliation of non-GAAP measures accompanying this release.&nbsp;&nbsp;See also &#8220;non-GAAP Financial Measures&#8221; below.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Hajime Uba, President and Chief Executive Officer of Kura Sushi, stated, &#8220;With the safety and well-being of our team members and guests as our top priority, we have taken all the necessary actions to adhere to CDC, state, and local guidelines, including temporarily closing all of our restaurants.&nbsp;&nbsp;During these trying times, we are fortunate to have a strong balance sheet with a cash and cash equivalents balance of approximately $24 million and no debt as of April 13, 2020.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our financial stability, combined with other steps we have taken to bolster our liquidity, gives us the confidence that we can weather these challenging economic conditions.&#8221;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Uba concluded, &#8220;We were pleased with our second quarter results as we posted double digit top line growth, an increase in comparable restaurant sales greater than 10%, and a modest improvement in our restaurant-level contribution margin.&nbsp;&nbsp;These strong results would not have been possible without the dedication of our hard-working team members, who we look forward to bringing back once we reopen our restaurants.&#8221; </p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU2"></a><font style="font-weight:bold;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">COVID-19 Business Update</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">As previously announced, on March 18, 2020, the Company temporarily closed all 25 of its restaurants and withdrew guidance for the fiscal year ending August 31, 2020, which was initially issued November 6, 2019.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company has since furloughed certain of its employees as a result of the restaurant closures, but will continue to provide health insurance benefits for furloughed employees. </p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The Company has a strong balance sheet with a cash and cash equivalents balance of approximately $24 million and no debt as of April 13, 2020.&nbsp;&nbsp;In order to preserve financial flexibility and conserve cash, while maintaining the near-term flexibility to re-open its restaurants efficiently when conditions allow, the Company has taken certain measures to reduce costs and capital expenditures.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">On April 10, 2020, Kura Sushi Japan, the Company&#8217;s controlling stockholder, has agreed to make available a $20 million revolving line of credit to Kura Sushi for a period of four years.&nbsp;&nbsp;Kura Sushi has not borrowed any amount against the available revolving line of credit.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The Company has also applied for a PPP loan under the CARES Act.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company intends to use any loan funds on expenditures that would maximize forgivability under the terms of the program.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company&#8217;s application is still pending and there is no certainty that its application will be approved or that, if granted, the loan will qualify for forgiveness, in whole or in part. </p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Review of Second Quarter 2020 Financial Results</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Total sales increased 28% to $19.4 million compared to $15.1 million in the second quarter of 2019.&nbsp;&nbsp;The increase was primarily driven by incremental revenue from the five new restaurants opened subsequent to the second quarter of fiscal 2019 and comparable restaurant sales growth of 10.8%.&nbsp;&nbsp; The comparable restaurant sales growth included a 5.6% increase in traffic and a 5.2% increase in average check. On a two-year basis, comparable restaurant sales growth was 17.6%.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Food and beverage costs were $6.1 million, representing a reduction as a percentage of sales of 60 basis points to 31.5%.&nbsp;&nbsp;This decrease was primarily driven by pricing, and to a lesser degree, reduced waste.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Labor and related costs were $6.1 million, representing a reduction as a percentage of sales of 50 basis points to 31.7%. This decrease was largely driven by pricing and more efficient staffing practices.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Occupancy and related expenses were $1.6 million, representing an increase as a percentage of sales of 130 basis points to 8.4%. This increase was primarily driven by higher occupancy rates in our newer restaurants and an increase in pre-opening lease expense.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">General and administrative costs increased by $1.0 million to $2.8 million, or 14.4% of sales. The increase was primarily due to $0.5 million of public company costs and $0.3 million in employee compensation related to additional headcount to support our growth in operations. </p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Operating loss was $0.2 million, compared to operating income of $0.3 million in the second quarter of 2019.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Net interest income during the first quarter was $137 thousand, compared to net interest expense of $35 thousand in the second quarter of 2019.  We currently have zero outstanding debt under our credit facilities.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Income tax expense was approximately $30 thousand compared to an expense of $35 thousand in the second quarter of 2019. </p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Net loss was $0.1 million, or ($0.02) per diluted share, compared to net income of $0.2 million, or $0.04 per diluted share, in the second quarter of 2019. </p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Restaurant-level contribution* was $3.9 million compared to $2.9 million in the second quarter of 2019.&nbsp;&nbsp;As a percentage of restaurant sales, restaurant-level contribution margin increased 80 basis points year-over-year to 20.1%.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Adjusted EBITDA* increased to $1.4 million compared to $1.2 million in the second quarter of 2019.</p>
<p style="text-align:right;margin-top:12pt;border-top:Solid 0.75pt #D9D9D9;padding-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">2</a><font style="font-weight:bold;"> | </font><font style="color:#7F7F7F;letter-spacing:3pt;">Page</font></p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU3"></a><font style="font-weight:bold;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Restaurant Development</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">During the second quarter of 2020, two new restaurants were opened in Katy, Texas and Glendale, California.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Fiscal Year 2020 Outlook</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">As previously announced, due to the ongoing uncertainty around the duration and severity of the COVID-19 pandemic, the Company has withdrawn its financial guidance for fiscal 2020, the period ending August 31, 2020.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Conference Call</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">A conference call and webcast to discuss Kura Sushi&#8217;s financial results is scheduled for 5:00 p.m. ET today. Hosting the conference call and webcast will be Hajime &#8220;Jimmy&#8221; Uba, President and Chief Executive Officer; Koji Shinohara, Chief Financial Officer; and Benjamin Porten, Investor Relations Manager.&nbsp;&nbsp; </p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Interested parties may listen to the conference call via telephone by dialing 201-689-8471. A telephone replay will be available shortly after the call has concluded and can be accessed by dialing 412-317-6671; the passcode is 13701829.&nbsp;&nbsp;The replay will be available until Tuesday, April 21, 2020.&nbsp;&nbsp;The webcast will be available at <font style="text-decoration:underline;">www.kurasushi.com</font> under the investor relations section and will be archived on the site shortly after the call has concluded.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:10pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">About Kura Sushi USA, Inc.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Kura Sushi USA, Inc. is a technology-enabled Japanese restaurant concept with 25 locations in five states. The Company offers guests a distinctive dining experience built on authentic Japanese cuisine and an engaging revolving sushi service model. Kura Sushi USA, Inc. was established in 2008 as a subsidiary of Kura Sushi, Inc., a Japan-based revolving sushi chain with over 400 restaurants and 35 years of brand history. For more information, please visit <font style="text-decoration:underline;">www.kurasushi.com</font>. </p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Key Financial Definitions</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Restaurant-level Contribution,<font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;"> a non-GAAP measure, is defined as operating income plus depreciation and amortization, stock-based compensation expense, pre-opening lease expense, pre-opening costs, non-cash lease expense and asset disposals, closure costs and restaurant impairments, general and administrative expenses, less corporate-level stock-based compensation expense and corporate-level pre-opening costs. Restaurant-level contribution margin is defined as restaurant-level contribution divided by sales.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">EBITDA,<font style="font-style:normal;"> </font><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;">a non-GAAP measure, is defined as net income (loss) before interest, income taxes and depreciation and amortization.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Adjusted EBITDA,<font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;"> a non-GAAP measure, is defined as EBITDA plus stock-based compensation expense, pre-opening lease expense, pre-opening costs, non-cash lease expense, asset disposals, closure costs and restaurant impairments, as well as certain items that the Company believes are not indicative of its core operating results. Adjusted EBITDA margin is defined as adjusted EBITDA divided by sales.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Comparable Restaurant Sales Growth<font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;"> refers to the change in year-over-year sales for the comparable restaurant base.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company include restaurants in the comparable restaurant base that have been in operation for at least 18 months prior to the start of the accounting period presented, including those temporarily closed for renovations during the year. For restaurants that were temporarily closed for renovations during the year, the Company makes fractional adjustments to sales such that sales are annualized in the associated period.&nbsp;&nbsp;Growth in comparable restaurant sales represents the percent change in sales from the same period in the prior year for the comparable restaurant base.&nbsp;&nbsp; </font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Non-GAAP Financial Measures</p>
<p style="margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:2.14%;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU4"></a>To supplement the condensed financial statements presented in accordance with U.S. generally accepted accounting principles (&#8220;GAAP&#8221;), certain financial measures, such as EBITDA, adjusted EBITDA, adjusted EBITDA margin, restaurant-level contribution and restaurant-level contribution margin (&#8220;Non-GAAP measures&#8221;) are not recognized under GAAP. These Non-GAAP measures are intended as supplemental measures of our performance that are neither required by, nor presented in accordance with, GAAP. The Company is presenting </p>
<p style="text-align:right;margin-top:12pt;border-top:Solid 0.75pt #D9D9D9;padding-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">3<font style="font-weight:bold;"> | </font><font style="color:#7F7F7F;letter-spacing:3pt;">Page</font></p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:2.14%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">these Non-GAAP measures because the C</font><font style="font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">ompany believes that they provide useful information to management and investors regarding certain financial and business trends relating to our financial condition and operating results. Addi</font><font style="font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">tionally, the Company presents restaurant-level c</font><font style="font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">ontribution because it excludes the impact of general and administrative expenses which are not incurred at the restaurant-level. </font><font style="font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The Company</font><font style="font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"> also use</font><font style="font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">s restaurant-level c</font><font style="font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">ontribution to measure operating performance and returns from opening new restaurants.</font></p>
<p style="margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:2.14%;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The Company believes that the use of these Non-GAAP measures provides an additional tool for investors to use in evaluating ongoing operating results and trends and in comparing the Company&#8217;s financial measures with those of comparable companies, which may present similar non-GAAP financial measures to investors. However, you should be aware that restaurant-level contribution and restaurant-level contribution margin are financial measures which are not indicative of overall results for the Company, and restaurant-level contribution and restaurant-level contribution margin do not accrue directly to the benefit of stockholders because of corporate-level expenses excluded from such measures. In addition, you should be aware when evaluating these Non-GAAP measures that in the future the Company may incur expenses similar to those excluded when calculating these measures. The Company&#8217;s presentation of these measures should not be construed as an inference that our future results will be unaffected by unusual or non-recurring items. Our computation of these Non-GAAP measures may not be comparable to other similarly titled measures computed by other companies, because all companies may not calculate these Non-GAAP measures in the same fashion. Because of these limitations, these Non-GAAP measures should not be considered in isolation or as a substitute for performance measures calculated in accordance with GAAP. The Company compensates for these limitations by relying primarily on our GAAP results and using these Non-GAAP measures on a supplemental basis. </p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Forward-Looking Statements</p>

These risks and uncertainties include but are not limited to: risks related to the COVID-19 outbreak; our ability to successfully maintain increases in our comparable restaurant sales; our ability to successfully execute our growth strategy and open new restaurants that are profitable; our ability to expand in existing and new markets; our projected growth in the number of our restaurants; macroeconomic conditions and other economic factors; our ability to compete with many other restaurants; our reliance on vendors, suppliers and distributors, including our parent company Kura Sushi, Inc.; concerns regarding food safety and foodborne illness; changes in consumer preferences and the level of acceptance of our restaurant concept in new markets; minimum wage increases and mandated employee benefits that could cause a significant increase in our labor costs; the failure of our automated equipment or information technology systems or the breach of our network security; the loss of key members of our management team; the impact of governmental laws and regulations; volatility in the price of our common stock; and other risks and uncertainties as described in our filings with the Securities and Exchange Commission (&#8220;SEC&#8221;).
